• Duration: ~6164s (1h42m11s suite runtime)
• Error: 1 blocking fail in openshift e2e suite — [sig-node] Pod InPlace Resize Container [FeatureGate:InPlacePodVerticalScaling] [Beta] test
• Evidence:

```

Blocking test failures:

* [sig-node] Pod InPlace Resize Container [FeatureGate:InPlacePodVerticalScaling] [Beta] Guaranteed QoS pod, three containers (c1, c2, c3) - increase: CPU (c1,c3), memory (c2, c3) ; decrease: CPU (c2)

Suite run returned error: 1 blocking fail, 0 informing fail, 1789 pass, 0 flaky, 2072 skip (1h42m11s)

```

The MonitorTest processed 119,234 intervals spanning 2026-06-21 13:15:44 to 2026-06-21 15:42:13, which includes the intentional SNO node reboot performed by the commatrix nftables test at 13:51:52:

```

2026/06/21 13:51:52 Node ip-10-0-104-6.ec2.internal is NotReady

```

• Root Cause: PROJECT TESTS PASSED — this failure is from the CI framework. The network-flow-matrix-tests step succeeded (finished.json: {"passed":true,"result":"SUCCESS"}). The commatrix nftables test intentionally rebooted the SNO node at 13:51 as part of its firewall-after-reboot verification. The subsequent standard OpenShift e2e suite (single-node-e2e-test step) caught a blocking failure in the unrelated [sig-node] InPlacePodVerticalScaling test. The "Node not ready" category reflects MonitorTest recording the intentional SNO reboot event (node was NotReady during commatrix test, before the e2e suite even started). The InPlace resize test failure on a post-reboot SNO node is a known flaky area; the node was rebooted at 13:51, the commatrix step finished at 13:59, and the e2e suite launched immediately after with potentially incomplete node recovery.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — likely a pre-existing flake in [sig-node] InPlacePodVerticalScaling on SNO with OCP 4.21; not related to any commatrix commit.
• Source File: [https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/release-4.21/test/e2e/nftables_test.go#L85](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/release-4.21/test/e2e/nftables_test.go#L85) (commatrix reboot trigger); the failing test itself is in the openshift-tests binary, not in commatrix source.
• Is it a flake? Yes — [sig-node] InPlacePodVerticalScaling tests are known to be flaky on SNO topologies, especially after a node reboot; the commatrix tests passed cleanly.
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job; the commatrix project tests are healthy. If the InPlace resize failure recurs consistently after an SNO reboot, open a sig-node issue or add a node stabilization wait between the commatrix step and the e2e suite.

TL;DR: Commatrix project tests passed; CI framework InPlacePodVerticalScaling sig-node test failed on post-reboot SNO.


Relation Between Failures: Both failures share a single root cause: the openshift e2e test binary (single-node-e2e-test step) exited with code 1 due to one blocking [sig-node] test failure. Test 2 is purely the ci-operator wrapping that exit code. The commatrix SNO reboot (intentional, part of nftables-after-reboot verification) finished cleanly before the e2e suite started, but the abbreviated node recovery window may have contributed to the InPlace resize test instability.


Per-Version Notes: OCP 4.21 nightly (2026-06-20-204857) — commatrix release-4.21 branch tests passed; failure is from platform e2e suite only.


Affected Images: registry.ci.openshift.org/ocp/release:4.21.0-0.nightly-2026-06-20-204857 (openshift-tests binary); commatrix test image is not implicated.

2026-06-21T13:00
❌ failure4.214.21-telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm127minfra_timeout MEDIUM
Bare-metal cluster API server unreachable; all 6 steps failed before commatrix tests ran.
7 failed tests
INFRA LOW

Full AI Analysis

Test 1: [network-flow-matrix-tests] network-flow-matrix-tests container test

• Duration: 1m43s
• Error: API server unreachable → get_cluster_version() returns . → git checkout release-. fails with pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

{"component":"entrypoint","error":"wrapped process failed: exit status 1",...}

```

• Root Cause: The test script's get_cluster_version() calls oc version | grep "Server Version:" | awk '{print $3}'. Because the bare metal cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64425 was unreachable (i/o timeout), oc version returns no server version — so major="", minor="", and echo "$major.$minor" returns . (a literal dot). This sets cluster_version="." and testing_branch="release-.", which does not exist in the repo. The cluster was healthy at setup completion (cnfdu18-master-0/1/2 all Ready, cluster version confirmed 4.21.0-0.nightly-2026-06-20-204857) but the API VIP became unreachable by the time the test pod launched — a transient bare metal network/infra failure.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — no code regression; the script robustness issue (no fallback to T5CI_VERSION=4.21 env var when server is unreachable) is a pre-existing fragility.
• Source File: [github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go) — test step script inlined in pod spec (not in commatrix repo; lives in openshift/release step registry).
• Is it a flake? yes — API server was healthy at cluster-setup completion, became unreachable transiently; this is characteristic of a bare metal network blip.
• Suggested Fix: In the CI step script, fall back to the T5CI_VERSION env var when oc version cannot reach the server (e.g., cluster_version="${T5CI_VERSION:-$(get_cluster_version)}" with a non-empty guard). Separately, retry or alert on job infra when the API is unreachable at test-phase start.


Test 2: [gather-must-gather] gather-must-gather container test

• Duration: 9m13s
• Error: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout — cannot reach API to run oc adm must-gather
• Evidence:

```

E0621 14:54:57.221799 55 memcache.go:265] "Unhandled Error" err="couldn't get current server API group list: Get \"https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=32s\": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout"

error completing cluster type inspection: error running backup collection: Get "https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=32s": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

error: creating temp namespace: Post "https://10.1.104.200:64425/api/v1/namespaces": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

```

• Root Cause: Same upstream cause as Test 1 — the cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64425 was unreachable. oc adm must-gather requires an API connection to inspect cluster state; it timed out after retrying for ~9 minutes.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra issue.
• Source File: CI step registry gather-must-gather (openshift/release).
• Is it a flake? yes — cascade from the API timeout infra failure.
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job; no code change needed in commatrix.

```
Unable to connect to the server: context deadline exceeded
```

• Evidence:

```

E0621 15:05:44.558879 45 memcache.go:265] "Unhandled Error" err="couldn't get current server API group list: Get \"https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=32s\": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout"
```

• Root Cause: Same as Test 1. Audit log collection requires API access; the ClusterVersion: Installing "" for and missing clusteroperators confirm the API server was not returning data for the entire post-phase duration (~20 minutes), consistent with a persistent network partition between the CI pod and the bare metal cluster.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra issue.
• Source File: CI step registry gather-audit-logs (openshift/release).
• Is it a flake? yes — cascade from API unreachable.
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job; no code change needed in commatrix.

• Duration: ~547s (9m7s)

• Root Cause: CI artifact-gather step gather-extra could not reach the cluster API server within its short 5-second timeout (repeated over ~25s before giving up). The cluster at 10.1.104.200:64416 was fully unresponsive, and gather-extra exited with code 1 after exhausting retries.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/gather-extra (CI framework step, not commatrix)

Baremetal cluster API server `10.1.104.200:64424` was unreachable; all steps timed out before any commatrix tests ran.

Full AI Analysis

Test 1: [network-flow-matrix-tests] network-flow-matrix-tests container test

• Duration: 1m43s
• Error: API server unreachable → get_cluster_version() returns . → git checkout release-. fails with pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

{"component":"entrypoint","error":"wrapped process failed: exit status 1",...}

```

• Root Cause: The test script's get_cluster_version() calls oc version | grep "Server Version:" | awk '{print $3}'. Because the bare metal cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64425 was unreachable (i/o timeout), oc version returns no server version — so major="", minor="", and echo "$major.$minor" returns . (a literal dot). This sets cluster_version="." and testing_branch="release-.", which does not exist in the repo. The cluster was healthy at setup completion (cnfdu18-master-0/1/2 all Ready, cluster version confirmed 4.21.0-0.nightly-2026-06-20-204857) but the API VIP became unreachable by the time the test pod launched — a transient bare metal network/infra failure.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — no code regression; the script robustness issue (no fallback to T5CI_VERSION=4.21 env var when server is unreachable) is a pre-existing fragility.
• Source File: [github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go) — test step script inlined in pod spec (not in commatrix repo; lives in openshift/release step registry).
• Is it a flake? yes — API server was healthy at cluster-setup completion, became unreachable transiently; this is characteristic of a bare metal network blip.
• Suggested Fix: In the CI step script, fall back to the T5CI_VERSION env var when oc version cannot reach the server (e.g., cluster_version="${T5CI_VERSION:-$(get_cluster_version)}" with a non-empty guard). Separately, retry or alert on job infra when the API is unreachable at test-phase start.


Test 2: [gather-must-gather] gather-must-gather container test

• Duration: 9m13s
• Error: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout — cannot reach API to run oc adm must-gather
• Evidence:

```

E0621 14:54:57.221799 55 memcache.go:265] "Unhandled Error" err="couldn't get current server API group list: Get \"https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=32s\": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout"

error completing cluster type inspection: error running backup collection: Get "https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=32s": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

error: creating temp namespace: Post "https://10.1.104.200:64425/api/v1/namespaces": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

```

Test 1: [network-flow-matrix-tests] network-flow-matrix-tests container test

• Duration: 1m43s
• Error: API server unreachable → get_cluster_version() returns . → git checkout release-. fails with pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

{"component":"entrypoint","error":"wrapped process failed: exit status 1",...}

```

• Root Cause: The test script's get_cluster_version() calls oc version | grep "Server Version:" | awk '{print $3}'. Because the bare metal cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64425 was unreachable (i/o timeout), oc version returns no server version — so major="", minor="", and echo "$major.$minor" returns . (a literal dot). This sets cluster_version="." and testing_branch="release-.", which does not exist in the repo. The cluster was healthy at setup completion (cnfdu18-master-0/1/2 all Ready, cluster version confirmed 4.21.0-0.nightly-2026-06-20-204857) but the API VIP became unreachable by the time the test pod launched — a transient bare metal network/infra failure.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — no code regression; the script robustness issue (no fallback to T5CI_VERSION=4.21 env var when server is unreachable) is a pre-existing fragility.
• Source File: [github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go) — test step script inlined in pod spec (not in commatrix repo; lives in openshift/release step registry).
• Is it a flake? yes — API server was healthy at cluster-setup completion, became unreachable transiently; this is characteristic of a bare metal network blip.
• Suggested Fix: In the CI step script, fall back to the T5CI_VERSION env var when oc version cannot reach the server (e.g., cluster_version="${T5CI_VERSION:-$(get_cluster_version)}" with a non-empty guard). Separately, retry or alert on job infra when the API is unreachable at test-phase start.

Now I have enough information to write the full analysis.



Test 1: [network-flow-matrix-tests] network-flow-matrix-tests container test

• Duration: ~67s
• Error: Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64416: i/o timeout
• Root Cause: The bare-metal cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64416 was completely unreachable when the test pod started. The oc client could not reach the cluster before any commatrix test code ran. A secondary error (error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git) shows the OCP version env var was empty/unset when the script tried to git checkout release-${OCP_VERSION}, meaning the cluster environment was never properly initialized.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss, not a code regression
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix (test entrypoint script, not commatrix Go code)
• Is it a flake? yes — bare-metal cluster became unreachable before test execution; commatrix tests never actually ran
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. If recurs, investigate bare-metal cluster cnfdu9 health and whether the API server recovers after reboot; also audit the OCP_VERSION variable substitution in the entrypoint script.


Test 2: [gather-must-gather] gather-must-gather container test

• Duration: ~547s (9m7s)
• Error: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64416: i/o timeout — oc adm must-gather could not reach cluster API
• Root Cause: This is a CI artifact-collection step (not a commatrix test). oc adm must-gather repeatedly failed to connect to 10.1.104.200:64416 over a 9-minute window. The cluster API was unreachable by the time this post-test step ran. This is a downstream symptom of the cluster losing connectivity.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/gather-must-gather (CI framework step, not commatrix)
• Is it a flake? yes — CI artifact-gather step failing solely because the cluster API server was unreachable
• Suggested Fix: No code change needed. Retry the job; investigate why the bare-metal cluster became unreachable during/after the test phase.


Test 3: [gather-extra] gather-extra container test

• Duration: ~31s
• Error: couldn't get current server API group list: Get "https://10.1.104.200:64416/api?timeout=5s": context deadline exceeded
• Root Cause: CI artifact-gather step gather-extra could not reach the cluster API server within its short 5-second timeout (repeated over ~25s before giving up). The cluster at 10.1.104.200:64416 was fully unresponsive, and gather-extra exited with code 1 after exhausting retries.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/gather-extra (CI framework step, not commatrix)
• Is it a flake? yes — cluster API unreachable; not related to commatrix code
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. The 31s failure indicates fast-fail on context deadline; if the cluster is healthy on retry this step will pass.


Test 4: [gather-audit-logs] gather-audit-logs container test

• Duration: ~547s (9m7s)
• Error: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64416: i/o timeout — oc adm inspect failed; cluster version and operators unreachable
• Root Cause: Audit-log collection (CI framework step) failed because the cluster API at 10.1.104.200:64416 was unreachable. Repeated 30-second timeout cycles are visible in the log. The reprinted cluster state shows ClusterOperators: clusteroperators are missing and error getting cluster version, confirming full API loss.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/gather-audit-logs (CI framework step, not commatrix)
• Is it a flake? yes — all errors are connectivity failures to the cluster API; no commatrix logic involved
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. Check bare-metal host cnfdu9 for power or network issues that could cause the API server to drop.


Test 5: [telco5g-log-gather] telco5g-log-gather container test

• Duration: ~70s (1m10s)
• Error: Container exited with code 1 after pip-install phase; log truncated mid-download of Python dependencies
• Root Cause: The telco5g-log-gather step began installing Python dependencies (requests, markupsafe, etc.) but the pod was killed/failed before completing. The log ends abruptly mid-pip-download, consistent with the broader cluster connectivity loss cutting off the pod's ability to communicate with or complete its work. No actual log-gather output was produced.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/telco5g-log-gather (CI framework step)
• Is it a flake? yes — pod terminated mid-execution due to infrastructure failure, not a script bug
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. If Python deps download is slow, consider pre-baking them into the step container image to reduce setup time.


Test 6: [unknown] Run multi-stage test test phase

• Duration: ~67s (1m7s, matching network-flow-matrix-tests pod)
• Error: "telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm" pod "telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm-network-flow-matrix-tests" failed: could not watch pod
• Root Cause: This is the ci-operator outer wrapper reporting the multi-stage test phase failure. It was unable to watch the network-flow-matrix-tests pod because the cluster API (10.1.104.200:64416) became unreachable. This entry is a duplicate/aggregate of Test 1 seen from the ci-operator perspective.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: sigs.k8s.io/prow/pkg/entrypoint/run.go:84 (Prow entrypoint, CI framework)
• Is it a flake? yes — ci-operator lost watch on the pod due to the same API server outage
• Suggested Fix: Same as Test 1 — retry the job; no commatrix code change needed.


TL;DR: Bare-metal cluster API server unreachable; all 6 steps failed before commatrix tests ran.


Relation Between Failures: All 6 failures share a single root cause: the bare-metal cluster cnfdu9's Kubernetes API server at 10.1.104.200:64416 became unreachable with I/O timeouts during or before the test phase. The network-flow-matrix-tests pod could not connect to the cluster, causing test abort; all subsequent gather/log steps then failed for the same reason. The secondary error: pathspec 'release-.' error in the test log indicates the OCP_VERSION environment variable was empty, which may indicate the cluster environment was never properly provisioned.


Per-Version Notes: OCP 4.22 — bare-metal cluster infra outage; no code-level regression identified on this version.


Affected Images: quay.io/openshift/origin-tests (gather steps), telco5g-log-gather image (Python-based), network-flow-matrix-tests image (go1.22.4/oc 4.12.29)

Test 1: network-flow-matrix-tests — network-flow-matrix-tests container test


• Duration: 70s
• Error: Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64424: i/o timeout + error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64424: i/o timeout

Go version: go version go1.22.4 linux/amd64

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

{"component":"entrypoint","error":"wrapped process failed: exit status 1",...}

```

• Root Cause: Two compounding failures. First, the target baremetal cluster API server (10.1.104.200:64424, cluster cnfdu17) was unreachable via TCP — every oc call timed out. Second, the test step script attempted git checkout release-. (a malformed branch), indicating the OCP version environment variable that builds the branch name (e.g. release-${OCP_VERSION}) was empty at runtime. Both failures cause exit status 1 before any commatrix test code ran. The git pathspec release-. is a distinct script/config bug unrelated to the cluster timeout.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — the git-checkout branch name issue may trace to the step config in openshift/release; no recent commatrix commit is implicated.
• Source File: [https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/tree/main/test/e2e](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/tree/main/test/e2e) (test never reached this code)
• Is it a flake? Partially — the cluster API timeout is an infra flake; the release-. pathspec error may be a persistent misconfiguration.
• Suggested Fix: Investigate why the baremetal cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64424 was unreachable at test time despite cluster-setup succeeding; separately audit the test step script in openshift/release to ensure the OCP version variable is correctly exported and non-empty before the git checkout release-${OCP_VERSION} call.

Relation Between Failures: All five "failed tests" are sequential retry iterations of the exact same Ansible task (Run oc command to check if cluster is ready) in ocp-install.yml within the telco5g-sno-setup step. They share a single root cause: the kube-apiserver at 192.168.17.114:6443 was unreachable with "no route to host" throughout the entire retry window. The downstream gather step failures (must-gather, gather-extra, gather-audit-logs, telco5g-log-gather) are secondary cascading failures from the same dead cluster.

• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — this is a test scheduling/sequencing issue in the job definition, not a code regression.

• Is it a flake? yes — the intentional node reboot is a documented side-effect of the nftables test; whether MonitorTest flags it depends on timing relative to the e2e suite's monitoring window.
• Suggested Fix: Ensure single-node-e2e-test runs before network-flow-matrix-tests in the job step ordering, or annotate the node-not-ready interval as expected/allowed in the MonitorTest configuration for this SNO upgrade job.

Full AI Analysis

Test 1: [TestE2e/Validation] should validate the communication matrix ports match the node's open ports

• Duration: 44.076s
• Error: the following ports are used but don't have an endpointslice: Ingress,TCP,40359,,crio,,,master,false
• Root Cause: CRI-O (container runtime) opened an ephemeral listening socket on TCP/40359 (Linux ephemeral range 32768–60999). filterOutPortsOfKnownServices() at validation_test.go:221 only skips rpc.statd, dnsmasq, and dig — not crio. filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges() only covers NodePort range 30000–32767 (KubeletNodePortDefaultDynamicRange), so 40359 is not filtered and the Fail() at line 161 is triggered.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — no code regression; crio was never added to the known-services filter, and this is a newly-observed ephemeral port binding by crio in OCP 4.23/5.0.
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/validation_test.go#L161
• Is it a flake? Yes — port 40359 is OS-assigned and changes each run; this specific port number is ephemeral but the underlying crio behavior may be consistent.
• Suggested Fix: Add crio to filterOutPortsOfKnownServices() in validation_test.go:221–238, analogous to how rpc.statd is handled, since crio's dynamically-bound sockets are host-level process ports with no Kubernetes EndpointSlice.


Test 2: [TestE2e] TestE2e

• Duration: 507.44s
• Error: --- FAIL: TestE2e (507.44s) — suite-level failure due to 1 failed spec
• Root Cause: TestE2e is the Go test function that runs the Ginkgo suite (test/e2e/). It fails because the child spec "should validate the communication matrix ports match the node's open ports" failed. The suite ran 4 of 4 specs; 3 passed, 1 failed. This is a cascading failure from Test 1 above.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — same root cause as Test 1.
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/validation_test.go
• Is it a flake? Same as Test 1 — conditional on crio binding an ephemeral port not covered by the filter.
• Suggested Fix: Same fix as Test 1; resolving the child spec failure resolves the suite.


Relation Between Failures: Both failures are the same root cause: a single failing Ginkgo It spec causes the parent TestE2e suite to fail. Port TCP/40359 is a crio-owned ephemeral socket that passes through all filters (filterOutPortsOfKnownServices and filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges) because crio is not in the known-services skip list and 40359 falls outside the NodePort dynamic range.


Per-Version Notes:

• OCP 4.23: Confirmed affected — this evidence run; crio opens TCP/40359 with no EndpointSlice.
• OCP 5.0: Also affected per the prompt; same root cause is expected since crio ephemeral port behavior is not version-specific to OCP.

Affected Images: quay.io/openshift-kni/commatrix (test container image built from the commatrix repo, run in the network-flow-matrix-tests step)


Overall Issue Class: matrix_mismatch


Overall Severity: MEDIUM — the test correctly identifies a real discrepancy (crio ephemeral port lacks EndpointSlice), but the fix is a test-side filter addition rather than a cluster misconfiguration; the cluster itself is functioning normally.

Test 1: [Validation] should validate the communication matrix ports match the node's open ports


• Duration: 20.809 seconds (within the 448.895s overall suite run)
• Error: the following ports are used but don't have an endpointslice: Ingress,TCP,44463,,crio,,,master,false — triggered at test/e2e/validation_test.go:161
• Root Cause: Port TCP 44463 is bound by the CRI-O container runtime process (pid=2677) as an ephemeral host-level socket (LISTEN 0 4096 10.0.82.179:44463 0.0.0.0:*). Because it is a host process, no Kubernetes EndpointSlice exists for it. Prior to PR #400, the generated commatrix.DynamicRanges included the Linux ephemeral private port range (32768–60999), and the call to filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges at validation_test.go:159 would have silently discarded port 44463 (which falls in that range). PR #400 removed getLinuxDynamicPrivateRange from pkg/dynamic-ranges/dynamic-ranges.go and deleted types.LinuxDynamicPrivateDefaultDynamicRange, leaving only the Kubernetes NodePort range (30000–32767) as a dynamic filter. Port 44463 is outside that range, and filterOutPortsOfKnownServices (validation_test.go:221–239) only exempts rpc.statd, dnsmasq, and dig — not crio — so the port survives all filtering and causes the Fail at line 161.
• Breaking PR/Commit: [PR #400 — "Remove Linux Dynamic ranges from generated communication matrix"](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/pull/400) — merged 2026-04-28, commit 7d56343e0d6e32f2fcc9b639ada47bb83cc57740. The specific change that broke the test was the deletion of LinuxDynamicPrivateDefaultDynamicRange from pkg/types/static-custom-entries.go and the removal of getLinuxDynamicPrivateRange from pkg/dynamic-ranges/dynamic-ranges.go, which together stripped the 32768–60999 dynamic-range filter from the validation path.
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/validation_test.go#L161
• Is it a flake? Likely yes for the specific port number, but structurally a deterministic regression. Port 44463 is an ephemeral OS-assigned port; on any given run the exact port number from CRI-O will differ, but CRI-O consistently opens an ephemeral host-level socket (for internal streaming/gRPC) that lands in the 32768–60999 range. Before PR #400, every such port was silently filtered. After PR #400, every run where CRI-O's ephemeral port lands outside 30000–32767 (i.e. practically every run) will fail. The failure mode is therefore structurally consistent, even if the exact port number varies per run.
• Suggested Fix: Add crio (and potentially any other known container-runtime host processes) to the filterOutPortsOfKnownServices function in test/e2e/validation_test.go, following the same pattern already used for rpc.statd (line 226–229). CRI-O is a host-level daemon that will never have an EndpointSlice; treating it exactly like rpc.statd is the correct semantic. A broader but also valid fix is to re-introduce the Linux ephemeral range as a separate, test-only filter (not in the firewall matrix), so any ephemeral host process is automatically excluded from the EPS validation without re-opening the firewall concern that motivated PR #400.


Relation Between Failures: There is only one failed test. The 6 ports reported as "in matrix but not in use" (TCP 80, 443, 8798, 9192 — in the documented aws-sno.csv but absent from EndpointSlices; TCP 9443, 10258 — in the generated EPS matrix but not open on the node) are logged as logrus.Warningf calls and do not cause a Fail. They are independent documentation drift issues (stale entries in docs/stable/raw/aws-sno.csv) unrelated to the single test failure.


Per-Version Notes: Only OCP 5.0 (periodic-ci-openshift-release-main-nightly-5.0-aws-ovn-network-flow-matrix-single-node) was examined. PR #400 targets the main branch, so any version tracking

Test 1: [TestE2e] Validation [It] should validate the communication matrix ports match the node's open ports


• Duration: 27.520 seconds (within the overall suite of 461.49s)

• Error:

```

the following ports are used but don't have an endpointslice:

Ingress,TCP,43067,,crio,,,master,false

Ingress,TCP,45329,,crio,,,master,false

Ingress,TCP,46203,,crio,,,master,false

Ingress,TCP,32911,,crio,,,worker,false

Ingress,TCP,33525,,crio,,,worker,false

Ingress,TCP,36315,,crio,,,worker,false

```

Assertion at test/e2e/validation_test.go:161 via Fail(...).


• Root Cause: PR #400 (commit 7d56343, merged 1fec55d on 2026-04-28) intentionally removed LinuxDynamicPrivateDefaultDynamicRange (TCP/UDP 32768–60999) from the generated commatrix's DynamicRanges. The test at validation_test.go:159 calls filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges(missingEPSMat, commatrix.DynamicRanges) to suppress ephemeral-port false positives before asserting. After the PR, commatrix.DynamicRanges only contains the NodePort range (30000–32767), so Linux ephemeral ports are no longer filtered. CRI-O binds random ephemeral TCP ports on the node IP (confirmed in raw-ss-tcp: e.g. 192.168.111.22:43067 ... crio,pid=2911); those ports have no Kubernetes EndpointSlice and now pass through to the Fail() call. The fix was intentional for nftables generation (opening the entire ephemeral range in a firewall is undesirable), but the test suppression was a side effect that was not replaced. The filterOutPortsOfKnownServices function at line 221–239 skips rpc.statd, dnsmasq, and dig, but crio is not included.

• Breaking PR/Commit: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/pull/400 — commit [7d56343](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/commit/7d56343e0d6e32f2fcc9b639ada47bb83cc57740) authored by Shir Moran, merged 2026-04-28.

• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/validation_test.go#L161

• Is it a flake? No. CRI-O consistently binds ephemeral TCP ports on node IPs on every cluster run (observed on master-0, master-2, worker-0, worker-1, worker-2 across all nodes in the raw-ss-tcp evidence). The port numbers change per run (ephemeral), but crio ports in 32768–60999 with no EndpointSlice will always appear. Every run since PR #400 merged will trigger this failure.

• Suggested Fix: Extend filterOutPortsOfKnownServices() in validation_test.go to also skip entries where Service == "crio" (matching the same pattern already used for rpc.statd). This is the minimal, targeted fix that doesn't reintroduce the broad ephemeral range into the generated matrix. Alternatively, a separate hardcoded LinuxEphemeralRange constant (32768–60999) could be used solely in this test's filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges call without adding it back to the generated commatrix, preserving the intentional firewall behavior of PR #400.


Relation Between Failures: There is only one failing test. The 7 stale-in-matrix ports (6388, 8798 ×2, 9192, 9443, 68/UDP ×2) are logged as warnings at validation_test.go:153–154 (logrus.Warningf) but do not trigger a Fail() — the test only asserts on ports that are open on nodes but missing an EndpointSlice, not the reverse. The single test failure is entirely caused by the 6 crio ephemeral ports losing their filter after PR #400.


Per-Version Notes:

• 4.23: Failing due to crio ephemeral ports in Linux range 32768–60999 no longer filtered (PR #400 on main). Evidence is from this version.
• 5.0: Same root cause. PR #400 was merged to main and the rename-tekton-pipelines-5-0 change (2a312c5) confirms the 5.0 branch tracks the same codebase. CRI-O ephemeral port behavior is identical across OCP versions, so the same filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges regression applies.

Test 1: [network-flow-matrix-tests] network-flow-matrix-tests container test

• Duration: 1m43s
• Error: API server unreachable → get_cluster_version() returns . → git checkout release-. fails with pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

{"component":"entrypoint","error":"wrapped process failed: exit status 1",...}

```

• Root Cause: The test script's get_cluster_version() calls oc version | grep "Server Version:" | awk '{print $3}'. Because the bare metal cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64425 was unreachable (i/o timeout), oc version returns no server version — so major="", minor="", and echo "$major.$minor" returns . (a literal dot). This sets cluster_version="." and testing_branch="release-.", which does not exist in the repo. The cluster was healthy at setup completion (cnfdu18-master-0/1/2 all Ready, cluster version confirmed 4.21.0-0.nightly-2026-06-20-204857) but the API VIP became unreachable by the time the test pod launched — a transient bare metal network/infra failure.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — no code regression; the script robustness issue (no fallback to T5CI_VERSION=4.21 env var when server is unreachable) is a pre-existing fragility.
• Source File: [github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go) — test step script inlined in pod spec (not in commatrix repo; lives in openshift/release step registry).
• Is it a flake? yes — API server was healthy at cluster-setup completion, became unreachable transiently; this is characteristic of a bare metal network blip.
• Suggested Fix: In the CI step script, fall back to the T5CI_VERSION env var when oc version cannot reach the server (e.g., cluster_version="${T5CI_VERSION:-$(get_cluster_version)}" with a non-empty guard). Separately, retry or alert on job infra when the API is unreachable at test-phase start.

Relation Between Failures: All 6 failures share a single



Test 1: [network-flow-matrix-tests] network-flow-matrix-tests container test

• Duration: 1m43s
• Error: API server unreachable → get_cluster_version() returns . → git checkout release-. fails with pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

{"component":"entrypoint","error":"wrapped process failed: exit status 1",...}

```

• Root Cause: The test script's get_cluster_version() calls oc version | grep "Server Version:" | awk '{print $3}'. Because the bare metal cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64425 was unreachable (i/o timeout), oc version returns no server version — so major="", minor="", and echo "$major.$minor" returns . (a literal dot). This sets cluster_version="." and testing_branch="release-.", which does not exist in the repo. The cluster was healthy at setup completion (cnfdu18-master-0/1/2 all Ready, cluster version confirmed 4.21.0-0.nightly-2026-06-20-204857) but the API VIP became unreachable by the time the test pod launched — a transient bare metal network/infra failure.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — no code regression; the script robustness issue (no fallback to T5CI_VERSION=4.21 env var when server is unreachable) is a pre-existing fragility.
• Source File: [github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go) — test step script inlined in pod spec (not in commatrix repo; lives in openshift/release step registry).
• Is it a flake? yes — API server was healthy at cluster-setup completion, became unreachable transiently; this is characteristic of a bare metal network blip.
• Suggested Fix: In the CI step script, fall back to the T5CI_VERSION env var when oc version cannot reach the server (e.g., cluster_version="${T5CI_VERSION:-$(get_cluster_version)}" with a non-empty guard). Separately, retry or alert on job infra when the API is unreachable at test-phase start.


Test 2: [gather-must-gather] gather-must-gather container test

• Duration: 9m13s
• Error: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout — cannot reach API to run oc adm must-gather
• Evidence:

```

E0621 14:54:57.221799 55 memcache.go:265] "Unhandled Error" err="couldn't get current server API group list: Get \"https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=32s\": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout"

error completing cluster type inspection: error running backup collection: Get "https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=32s": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

error: creating temp namespace: Post "https://10.1.104.200:64425/api/v1/namespaces": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

```

• Root Cause: Same upstream cause as Test 1 — the cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64425 was unreachable. oc adm must-gather requires an API connection to inspect cluster state; it timed out after retrying for ~9 minutes.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra issue.
• Source File: CI step registry gather-must-gather (openshift/release).
• Is it a flake? yes — cascade from the API timeout infra failure.
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job; no code change needed in commatrix.


Test 3: [gather-extra] gather-extra container test

• Duration: 30s
• Error: context deadline exceeded — oc cannot reach API server at 10.1.104.200:64425
• Evidence:

```

Gathering artifacts ...

E0621 14:58:12.479071 28 memcache.go:265] "Unhandled Error" err="couldn't get current server API group list: Get \"https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=5s\": context deadline exceeded"

Unable to connect to the server: context deadline exceeded

```

• Root Cause: Same as Test 1 — cluster API unreachable. gather-extra failed almost instantly (30s) because it hit a hard context deadline exceeded rather than TCP-level i/o timeout.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra issue.
• Source File: CI step registry gather-extra (openshift/release).
• Is it a flake? yes — cascade from API unreachable.
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job; no code change needed in commatrix.

Audit log collection requires API access; the ClusterVersion: Installing "" for and missing clusteroperators confirm the API server was not returning data for the entire post-phase duration (~20 minutes), consistent with a persistent network partition between the CI pod and the bare metal cluster.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra issue.

Now I have enough information to write the full analysis.



Test 1: [network-flow-matrix-tests] network-flow-matrix-tests container test

• Duration: ~67s
• Error: Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64416: i/o timeout
• Root Cause: The bare-metal cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64416 was completely unreachable when the test pod started. The oc client could not reach the cluster before any commatrix test code ran. A secondary error (error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git) shows the OCP version env var was empty/unset when the script tried to git checkout release-${OCP_VERSION}, meaning the cluster environment was never properly initialized.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss, not a code regression
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix (test entrypoint script, not commatrix Go code)
• Is it a flake? yes — bare-metal cluster became unreachable before test execution; commatrix tests never actually ran
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. If recurs, investigate bare-metal cluster cnfdu9 health and whether the API server recovers after reboot; also audit the OCP_VERSION variable substitution in the entrypoint script.


Test 2: [gather-must-gather] gather-must-gather container test

• Duration: ~547s (9m7s)
• Error: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64416: i/o timeout — oc adm must-gather could not reach cluster API
• Root Cause: This is a CI artifact-collection step (not a commatrix test). oc adm must-gather repeatedly failed to connect to 10.1.104.200:64416 over a 9-minute window. The cluster API was unreachable by the time this post-test step ran. This is a downstream symptom of the cluster losing connectivity.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/gather-must-gather (CI framework step, not commatrix)
• Is it a flake? yes — CI artifact-gather step failing solely because the cluster API server was unreachable
• Suggested Fix: No code change needed. Retry the job; investigate why the bare-metal cluster became unreachable during/after the test phase.


Test 3: [gather-extra] gather-extra container test

• Duration: ~31s
• Error: couldn't get current server API group list: Get "https://10.1.104.200:64416/api?timeout=5s": context deadline exceeded
• Root Cause: CI artifact-gather step gather-extra could not reach the cluster API server within its short 5-second timeout (repeated over ~25s before giving up). The cluster at 10.1.104.200:64416 was fully unresponsive, and gather-extra exited with code 1 after exhausting retries.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/gather-extra (CI framework step, not commatrix)
• Is it a flake? yes — cluster API unreachable; not related to commatrix code
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. The 31s failure indicates fast-fail on context deadline; if the cluster is healthy on retry this step will pass.


Test 4: [gather-audit-logs] gather-audit-logs container test

• Duration: ~547s (9m7s)
• Error: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64416: i/o timeout — oc adm inspect failed; cluster version and operators unreachable
• Root Cause: Audit-log collection (CI framework step) failed because the cluster API at 10.1.104.200:64416 was unreachable. Repeated 30-second timeout cycles are visible in the log. The reprinted cluster state shows ClusterOperators: clusteroperators are missing and error getting cluster version, confirming full API loss.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/gather-audit-logs (CI framework step, not commatrix)
• Is it a flake? yes — all errors are connectivity failures to the cluster API; no commatrix logic involved
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. Check bare-metal host cnfdu9 for power or network issues that could cause the API server to drop.


Test 5: [telco5g-log-gather] telco5g-log-gather container test

• Duration: ~70s (1m10s)
• Error: Container exited with code 1 after pip-install phase; log truncated mid-download of Python dependencies
• Root Cause: The telco5g-log-gather step began installing Python dependencies (requests, markupsafe, etc.) but the pod was killed/failed before completing. The log ends abruptly mid-pip-download, consistent with the broader cluster connectivity loss cutting off the pod's ability to communicate with or complete its work. No actual log-gather output was produced.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/telco5g-log-gather (CI framework step)
• Is it a flake? yes — pod terminated mid-execution due to infrastructure failure, not a script bug
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. If Python deps download is slow, consider pre-baking them into the step container image to reduce setup time.


Test 6: [unknown] Run multi-stage test test phase

• Duration: ~67s (1m7s, matching network-flow-matrix-tests pod)
• Error: "telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm" pod "telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm-network-flow-matrix-tests" failed: could not watch pod
• Root Cause: This is the ci-operator outer wrapper reporting the multi-stage test phase failure. It was unable to watch the network-flow-matrix-tests pod because the cluster API (10.1.104.200:64416) became unreachable. This entry is a duplicate/aggregate of Test 1 seen from the ci-operator perspective.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: sigs.k8s.io/prow/pkg/entrypoint/run.go:84 (Prow entrypoint, CI framework)
• Is it a flake? yes — ci-operator lost watch on the pod due to the same API server outage
• Suggested Fix: Same as Test 1 — retry the job; no commatrix code change needed.


TL;DR: Bare-metal cluster API server unreachable; all 6 steps failed before commatrix tests ran.


Relation Between Failures: All 6 failures share a single root cause: the bare-metal cluster cnfdu9's Kubernetes API server at 10.1.104.200:64416 became unreachable with I/O timeouts during or before the test phase. The network-flow-matrix-tests pod could not connect to the cluster, causing test abort; all subsequent gather/log steps then failed for the same reason. The secondary error: pathspec 'release-.' error in the test log indicates the OCP_VERSION environment variable was empty, which may indicate the cluster environment was never properly provisioned.


Per-Version Notes: OCP 4.22 — bare-metal cluster infra outage; no code-level regression identified on this version.


Affected Images: quay.io/openshift/origin-tests (gather steps), telco5g-log-gather image (Python-based), network-flow-matrix-tests image (go1.22.4/oc 4.12.29)


Overall Issue Class: infra_timeout


Overall Severity: MEDIUM

• Root Cause: Audit-log collection (CI framework step) failed because the cluster API at 10.1.104.200:64416 was unreachable. Repeated 30-second timeout cycles are visible in the log. The reprinted cluster state shows ClusterOperators: clusteroperators are missing and error getting cluster version, confirming full API loss.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/gather-audit-logs (CI framework step, not commatrix)
• Is it a flake? yes — all errors are connectivity failures to the cluster API; no commatrix logic involved
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. Check bare-metal host cnfdu9 for power or network issues that could cause the API server to drop.


Test 5: [telco5g-log-gather] telco5g-log-gather container test

• Duration: ~70s (1m10s)
• Error: Container exited with code 1 after pip-install phase; log truncated mid-download of Python dependencies
• Root Cause: The telco5g-log-gather step began installing Python dependencies (requests, markupsafe, etc.) but the pod was killed/failed before completing. The log ends abruptly mid-pip-download, consistent with the broader cluster connectivity loss cutting off the pod's ability to communicate with or complete its work. No actual log-gather output was produced.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra cluster loss
• Source File: https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/telco5g-log-gather (CI framework step)
• Is it a flake? yes — pod terminated mid-execution due to infrastructure failure, not a script bug
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. If Python deps download is slow, consider pre-baking them into the step container image to reduce setup time.


Test 6: [unknown] Run multi-stage test test phase

• Duration: ~67s (1m7s, matching network-flow-matrix-tests pod)
• Error: "telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm" pod "telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm-network-flow-matrix-tests" failed: could not watch pod
• Root Cause: This is the ci-operator outer wrapper reporting the multi-stage test phase failure. It was unable to watch the network-flow-matrix-tests pod because the cluster API (10.1.104.200:64416) became unreachable. This entry is a duplicate/aggregate of Test 1 seen from the ci-operator perspective.

TL;DR: Bare-metal cluster API server unreachable; all 6 steps failed before commatrix tests ran.


Relation Between Failures: All 6 failures share a single root cause: the bare-metal cluster cnfdu9's Kubernetes API server at 10.1.104.200:64416 became unreachable with I/O timeouts during or before the test phase. The network-flow-matrix-tests pod could not connect to the cluster, causing test abort; all subsequent gather/log steps then failed for the same reason. The secondary error: pathspec 'release-.' error in the test log indicates the OCP_VERSION environment variable was empty, which may indicate the cluster environment was never properly provisioned.


Per-Version Notes: OCP 4.22 — bare-metal cluster infra outage; no code-level regression identified on this version.


Affected Images: quay.io/openshift/origin-tests (gather steps), telco5g-log-gather image (Python-based), network-flow-matrix-tests image (go1.22.4/oc 4.12.29)

Test 1: [telco5g-sno-setup] RETRYING: [XXXXXXXXXXXX]: Run oc command to check if cluster is ready (60 retries left).

• Duration: ~9209s (2h33m49s total for the setup step)
• Error: OCP API server unreachable — dial tcp 192.168.17.114:6443: connect: no route to host
• Evidence:

> E0617 12:02:25.092451 3747229 memcache.go:265] couldn't get current server API group list: Get "https://api.cnfdu7.upstreamci.bos2.lab:6443/api?timeout=32s": dial tcp 192.168.17.114:6443: connect: no route to host

> PLAY RECAP: XXXXXXXXXXXX: ok=0 changed=0 unreachable=0 failed=1 skipped=0 rescued=0 ignored=0

• Root Cause: The bare-metal SNO node for cluster cnfdu7 failed to complete OCP installation. After ~2.5 hours, the ocp-install.yml Ansible playbook's cluster-readiness oc check hit "no route to host" on the kube-apiserver (192.168.17.114:6443), indicating the node lost network routing or the OCP bootstrap/install process failed before the API came up. This is a hardware/infra-level failure in the telco5g lab, not a commatrix code issue.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra failure, no code involved
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix (commatrix tests never ran)
• Is it a flake? yes — SNO bare-metal install failures due to routing loss are known transient lab infrastructure issues
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. If persistent, investigate the bare-metal node cnfdu7 for network/BMC issues and confirm the SNO installer can reach the bootstrap host.

They share a single root cause: the kube-apiserver at 192.168.17.114:6443 was unreachable with "no route to host" throughout the entire retry window. The downstream gather step failures (must-gather, gather-extra, gather-audit-logs, telco5g-log-gather) are secondary cascading failures from the same dead cluster.

Test 1: [TestE2e/Validation] should validate the communication matrix ports match the node's open ports

• Duration: 44.076s
• Error: the following ports are used but don't have an endpointslice: Ingress,TCP,40359,,crio,,,master,false
• Root Cause: CRI-O (container runtime) opened an ephemeral listening socket on TCP/40359 (Linux ephemeral range 32768–60999). filterOutPortsOfKnownServices() at validation_test.go:221 only skips rpc.statd, dnsmasq, and dig — not crio. filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges() only covers NodePort range 30000–32767 (KubeletNodePortDefaultDynamicRange), so 40359 is not filtered and the Fail() at line 161 is triggered.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — no code regression; crio was never added to the known-services filter, and this is a newly-observed ephemeral port binding by crio in OCP 4.23/5.0.
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/validation_test.go#L161
• Is it a flake? Yes — port 40359 is OS-assigned and changes each run; this specific port number is ephemeral but the underlying crio behavior may be consistent.
• Suggested Fix: Add crio to filterOutPortsOfKnownServices() in validation_test.go:221–238, analogous to how rpc.statd is handled, since crio's dynamically-bound sockets are host-level process ports with no Kubernetes EndpointSlice.


Test 2: [TestE2e] TestE2e

• Duration: 507.44s
• Error: --- FAIL: TestE2e (507.44s) — suite-level failure due to 1 failed spec
• Root Cause: TestE2e is the Go test function that runs the Ginkgo suite (test/e2e/). It fails because the child spec "should validate the communication matrix ports match the node's open ports" failed. The suite ran 4 of 4 specs; 3 passed, 1 failed. This is a cascading failure from Test 1 above.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — same root cause as Test 1.
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/validation_test.go
• Is it a flake? Same as Test 1 — conditional on crio binding an ephemeral port not covered by the filter.
• Suggested Fix: Same fix as Test 1; resolving the child spec failure resolves the suite.


Relation Between Failures: Both failures are the same root cause: a single failing Ginkgo It spec causes the parent TestE2e suite to fail. Port TCP/40359 is a crio-owned ephemeral socket that passes through all filters (filterOutPortsOfKnownServices and filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges) because crio is not in the known-services skip list and 40359 falls outside the NodePort dynamic range.

Test 1: [Validation] should validate the communication matrix ports match the node's open ports


• Duration: 20.809 seconds (within the 448.895s overall suite run)
• Error: the following ports are used but don't have an endpointslice: Ingress,TCP,44463,,crio,,,master,false — triggered at test/e2e/validation_test.go:161
• Root Cause: Port TCP 44463 is bound by the CRI-O container runtime process (pid=2677) as an ephemeral host-level socket (LISTEN 0 4096 10.0.82.179:44463 0.0.0.0:*). Because it is a host process, no Kubernetes EndpointSlice exists for it. Prior to PR #400, the generated commatrix.DynamicRanges included the Linux ephemeral private port range (32768–60999), and the call to filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges at validation_test.go:159 would have silently discarded port 44463 (which falls in that range). PR #400 removed getLinuxDynamicPrivateRange from pkg/dynamic-ranges/dynamic-ranges.go and deleted types.LinuxDynamicPrivateDefaultDynamicRange, leaving only the Kubernetes NodePort range (30000–32767) as a dynamic filter. Port 44463 is outside that range, and filterOutPortsOfKnownServices (validation_test.go:221–239) only exempts rpc.statd, dnsmasq, and dig — not crio — so the port survives all filtering and causes the Fail at line 161.
• Breaking PR/Commit: [PR #400 — "Remove Linux Dynamic ranges from generated communication matrix"](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/pull/400) — merged 2026-04-28, commit 7d56343e0d6e32f2fcc9b639ada47bb83cc57740. The specific change that broke the test was the deletion of LinuxDynamicPrivateDefaultDynamicRange from pkg/types/static-custom-entries.go and the removal of getLinuxDynamicPrivateRange from pkg/dynamic-ranges/dynamic-ranges.go, which together stripped the 32768–60999 dynamic-range filter from the validation path.
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/validation_test.go#L161
• Is it a flake? Likely yes for the specific port number, but structurally a deterministic regression. Port 44463 is an ephemeral OS-assigned port; on any given run the exact port number from CRI-O will differ, but CRI-O consistently opens an ephemeral host-level socket (for internal streaming/gRPC) that lands in the 32768–60999 range. Before PR #400, every such port was silently filtered. After PR #400, every run where CRI-O's ephemeral port lands outside 30000–32767 (i.e. practically every run) will fail. The failure mode is therefore structurally consistent, even if the exact port number varies per run.
• Suggested Fix: Add crio (and potentially any other known container-runtime host processes) to the filterOutPortsOfKnownServices function in test/e2e/validation_test.go, following the same pattern already used for rpc.statd (line 226–229). CRI-O is a host-level daemon that will never have an EndpointSlice; treating it exactly like rpc.statd is the correct semantic. A broader but also valid fix is to re-introduce the Linux ephemeral range as a separate, test-only filter (not in the firewall matrix), so any ephemeral host process is automatically excluded from the EPS validation without re-opening the firewall concern that motivated PR #400.


Relation Between Failures: There is only one failed test. The 6 ports reported as "in matrix but not in use" (TCP 80, 443, 8798, 9192 — in the documented aws-sno.csv but absent from EndpointSlices; TCP 9443, 10258 — in the generated EPS matrix but not open on the node) are logged as logrus.Warningf calls and do not cause a Fail. They are independent documentation drift issues (stale entries in docs/stable/raw/aws-sno.csv) unrelated to the single test failure.


Per-Version Notes: Only OCP 5.0 (periodic-ci-openshift-release-main-nightly-5.0-aws-ovn-network-flow-matrix-single-node) was examined. PR #400 targets the main branch, so any version tracking



Now I have all the information I need. Let me write the final analysis:

Test 1: [TestE2e] Validation [It] should validate the communication matrix ports match the node's open ports


• Duration: 27.520 seconds (within the overall suite of 461.49s)

• Error:

```

the following ports are used but don't have an endpointslice:

Ingress,TCP,43067,,crio,,,master,false

Ingress,TCP,45329,,crio,,,master,false

Ingress,TCP,46203,,crio,,,master,false

Ingress,TCP,32911,,crio,,,worker,false

Ingress,TCP,33525,,crio,,,worker,false

Ingress,TCP,36315,,crio,,,worker,false

```

Assertion at test/e2e/validation_test.go:161 via Fail(...).


• Root Cause: PR #400 (commit 7d56343, merged 1fec55d on 2026-04-28) intentionally removed LinuxDynamicPrivateDefaultDynamicRange (TCP/UDP 32768–60999) from the generated commatrix's DynamicRanges. The test at validation_test.go:159 calls filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges(missingEPSMat, commatrix.DynamicRanges) to suppress ephemeral-port false positives before asserting. After the PR, commatrix.DynamicRanges only contains the NodePort range (30000–32767), so Linux ephemeral ports are no longer filtered. CRI-O binds random ephemeral TCP ports on the node IP (confirmed in raw-ss-tcp: e.g. 192.168.111.22:43067 ... crio,pid=2911); those ports have no Kubernetes EndpointSlice and now pass through to the Fail() call. The fix was intentional for nftables generation (opening the entire ephemeral range in a firewall is undesirable), but the test suppression was a side effect that was not replaced. The filterOutPortsOfKnownServices function at line 221–239 skips rpc.statd, dnsmasq, and dig, but crio is not included.

• Breaking PR/Commit: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/pull/400 — commit [7d56343](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/commit/7d56343e0d6e32f2fcc9b639ada47bb83cc57740) authored by Shir Moran, merged 2026-04-28.

• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/validation_test.go#L161

• Is it a flake? No. CRI-O consistently binds ephemeral TCP ports on node IPs on every cluster run (observed on master-0, master-2, worker-0, worker-1, worker-2 across all nodes in the raw-ss-tcp evidence). The port numbers change per run (ephemeral), but crio ports in 32768–60999 with no EndpointSlice will always appear. Every run since PR #400 merged will trigger this failure.

• Suggested Fix: Extend filterOutPortsOfKnownServices() in validation_test.go to also skip entries where Service == "crio" (matching the same pattern already used for rpc.statd). This is the minimal, targeted fix that doesn't reintroduce the broad ephemeral range into the generated matrix. Alternatively, a separate hardcoded LinuxEphemeralRange constant (32768–60999) could be used solely in this test's filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges call without adding it back to the generated commatrix, preserving the intentional firewall behavior of PR #400.


Relation Between Failures: There is only one failing test. The 7 stale-in-matrix ports (6388, 8798 ×2, 9192, 9443, 68/UDP ×2) are logged as warnings at validation_test.go:153–154 (logrus.Warningf) but do not trigger a Fail() — the test only asserts on ports that are open on nodes but missing an EndpointSlice, not the reverse. The single test failure is entirely caused by the 6 crio ephemeral ports losing their filter after PR #400.


Per-Version Notes:

• 4.23: Failing due to crio ephemeral ports in Linux range 32768–60999 no longer filtered (PR #400 on main). Evidence is from this version.
• 5.0: Same root cause. PR #400 was merged to main and the rename-tekton-pipelines-5-0 change (2a312c5) confirms the 5.0 branch tracks the same codebase. CRI-O ephemeral port behavior is identical across OCP versions, so the same filterOutPortsInDynamicRanges regression applies.

• `registry.ci.openshift.org

Test 1: [network-flow-matrix-tests] network-flow-matrix-tests container test

• Duration: 1m43s
• Error: API server unreachable → get_cluster_version() returns . → git checkout release-. fails with pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

{"component":"entrypoint","error":"wrapped process failed: exit status 1",...}

```

• Root Cause: The test script's get_cluster_version() calls oc version | grep "Server Version:" | awk '{print $3}'. Because the bare metal cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64425 was unreachable (i/o timeout), oc version returns no server version — so major="", minor="", and echo "$major.$minor" returns . (a literal dot). This sets cluster_version="." and testing_branch="release-.", which does not exist in the repo. The cluster was healthy at setup completion (cnfdu18-master-0/1/2 all Ready, cluster version confirmed 4.21.0-0.nightly-2026-06-20-204857) but the API VIP became unreachable by the time the test pod launched — a transient bare metal network/infra failure.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — no code regression; the script robustness issue (no fallback to T5CI_VERSION=4.21 env var when server is unreachable) is a pre-existing fragility.
• Source File: [github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go) — test step script inlined in pod spec (not in commatrix repo; lives in openshift/release step registry).
• Is it a flake? yes — API server was healthy at cluster-setup completion, became unreachable transiently; this is characteristic of a bare metal network blip.
• Suggested Fix: In the CI step script, fall back to the T5CI_VERSION env var when oc version cannot reach the server (e.g., cluster_version="${T5CI_VERSION:-$(get_cluster_version)}" with a non-empty guard). Separately, retry or alert on job infra when the API is unreachable at test-phase start.

• Source File: [github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go) — test step script inlined in pod spec (not in commatrix repo; lives in openshift/release step registry).
• Is it a flake? yes — API server was healthy at cluster-setup completion, became unreachable transiently; this is characteristic of a bare metal network blip.
• Suggested Fix: In the CI step script, fall back to the T5CI_VERSION env var when oc version cannot reach the server (e.g., cluster_version="${T5CI_VERSION:-$(get_cluster_version)}" with a non-empty guard). Separately, retry or alert on job infra when the API is unreachable at test-phase start.

Test 4: [network-flow-matrix-tests] Run multi-stage test telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm - container test

• Duration: 1m11s
• Error: Two independent failures: (1) cluster API timeout, (2) invalid git branch release-.
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64414: i/o timeout

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

{"component":"entrypoint","error":"wrapped process failed: exit status 1",...}

```

• Root Cause: The test script fails at two points. First, the cluster API at 10.1.104.200:64414 was unreachable via i/o timeout before any test could run. Second, after cloning the commatrix repo, the script attempted git checkout release-. — a malformed branch name. The commatrix repo has only a main branch (confirmed by the local clone at /private/tmp/ci-investigate; git branch -r shows only origin/main). The branch name release-. is the result of a version variable evaluating to an empty string or just . in the CI script (expected: release-5.0). The entrypoint exits with code 1 from the git failure, preventing any commatrix tests from executing.
• Breaking PR/Commit: The git pathspec bug may be related to a CI config change in openshift/release — the variable that should expand to 5.0 is not being passed or is resolving incorrectly. Unknown specific commit.
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go (test entrypoint); CI runner script in openshift/release step registry.
• Is it a flake? No for the git checkout bug — release-. is a deterministic misconfiguration. Yes for the cluster API timeout — that is infrastructure noise.
• Suggested Fix: Fix the CI step script to correctly pass the OCP version (e.g., 5.0) into the git branch name variable so release-${OCP_VERSION} expands to release-5.0. Separately, confirm release-5.0 branch exists in the commatrix repo, or adjust the script to use main for trunk testing.

Test 1: [network-flow-matrix-tests] network-flow-matrix-tests container test

• Duration: 1m43s
• Error: API server unreachable → get_cluster_version() returns . → git checkout release-. fails with pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

{"component":"entrypoint","error":"wrapped process failed: exit status 1",...}

```

• Root Cause: The test script's get_cluster_version() calls oc version | grep "Server Version:" | awk '{print $3}'. Because the bare metal cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64425 was unreachable (i/o timeout), oc version returns no server version — so major="", minor="", and echo "$major.$minor" returns . (a literal dot). This sets cluster_version="." and testing_branch="release-.", which does not exist in the repo. The cluster was healthy at setup completion (cnfdu18-master-0/1/2 all Ready, cluster version confirmed 4.21.0-0.nightly-2026-06-20-204857) but the API VIP became unreachable by the time the test pod launched — a transient bare metal network/infra failure.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — no code regression; the script robustness issue (no fallback to T5CI_VERSION=4.21 env var when server is unreachable) is a pre-existing fragility.
• Source File: [github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/e2e_suite_test.go) — test step script inlined in pod spec (not in commatrix repo; lives in openshift/release step registry).
• Is it a flake? yes — API server was healthy at cluster-setup completion, became unreachable transiently; this is characteristic of a bare metal network blip.
• Suggested Fix: In the CI step script, fall back to the T5CI_VERSION env var when oc version cannot reach the server (e.g., cluster_version="${T5CI_VERSION:-$(get_cluster_version)}" with a non-empty guard). Separately, retry or alert on job infra when the API is unreachable at test-phase start.


Test 2: [gather-must-gather] gather-must-gather container test

• Duration: 9m13s
• Error: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout — cannot reach API to run oc adm must-gather
• Evidence:

```

E0621 14:54:57.221799 55 memcache.go:265] "Unhandled Error" err="couldn't get current server API group list: Get \"https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=32s\": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout"

error completing cluster type inspection: error running backup collection: Get "https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=32s": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

error: creating temp namespace: Post "https://10.1.104.200:64425/api/v1/namespaces": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

```

• Root Cause: Same upstream cause as Test 1 — the cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64425 was unreachable. oc adm must-gather requires an API connection to inspect cluster state; it timed out after retrying for ~9 minutes.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra issue.
• Source File: CI step registry gather-must-gather (openshift/release).
• Is it a flake? yes — cascade from the API timeout infra failure.
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job; no code change needed in commatrix.


Test 3: [gather-extra] gather-extra container test

• Duration: 30s
• Error: context deadline exceeded — oc cannot reach API server at 10.1.104.200:64425
• Evidence:

```

Gathering artifacts ...

E0621 14:58:12.479071 28 memcache.go:265] "Unhandled Error" err="couldn't get current server API group list: Get \"https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=5s\": context deadline exceeded"

Unable to connect to the server: context deadline exceeded

```

• Root Cause: Same as Test 1 — cluster API unreachable. gather-extra failed almost instantly (30s) because it hit a hard context deadline exceeded rather than TCP-level i/o timeout.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra issue.
• Source File: CI step registry gather-extra (openshift/release).
• Is it a flake? yes — cascade from API unreachable.
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job; no code change needed in commatrix.


Test 4: [gather-audit-logs] gather-audit-logs container test

• Duration: 9m10s
• Error: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout on repeated API calls; error getting cluster version: ... i/o timeout
• Evidence:

```

E0621 15:05:44.558879 45 memcache.go:265] "Unhandled Error" err="couldn't get current server API group list: Get \"https://10.1.104.200:64425/api?timeout=32s\": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout"

error getting cluster version: Get "https://10.1.104.200:64425/apis/config.openshift.io/v1/clusterversions/version": dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

ClusterVersion: Installing "" for :

clusteroperators are missing

```

• Root Cause: Same as Test 1. Audit log collection requires API access; the ClusterVersion: Installing "" for and missing clusteroperators confirm the API server was not returning data for the entire post-phase duration (~20 minutes), consistent with a persistent network partition between the CI pod and the bare metal cluster.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra issue.
• Source File: CI step registry gather-audit-logs (openshift/release).
• Is it a flake? yes — cascade from API unreachable.
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job; no code change needed in commatrix.


Test 5: [telco5g-log-gather] telco5g-log-gather container test

• Duration: 1m10s
• Error: Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout
• Evidence:

```

OC client version from the container:

Client Version: 4.12.29

Kustomize Version: v4.5.7

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64425: i/o timeout

```

• Root Cause: Same as Test 1 — cluster API server unreachable. telco5g-log-gather runs oc to collect logs; it immediately fails with the same i/o timeout. The step completed the python/pip install (no cluster access needed) but failed when trying to pull cluster logs.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra issue.
• Source File: CI step registry telco5g-log-gather (openshift/release).
• Is it a flake? yes — cascade from API unreachable.
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job; no code change needed in commatrix.


Test 6: [unknown] Run multi-stage test test phase

• Duration: 1m39s
• Error: pod "telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm-network-flow-matrix-tests" failed: could not watch pod: the pod ci-op-1kgnsp84/telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm-network-flow-matrix-tests failed after 1m39s (failed containers: test): ContainerFailed
• Evidence:

```

"telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm" pod "telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm-network-flow-matrix-tests" failed:

could not watch pod: the pod ci-op-1kgnsp84/telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm-network-flow-matrix-tests

failed after 1m39s (failed containers: test): ContainerFailed one or more containers exited

Container test exited with code 1, reason Error

```

• Root Cause: This is the ci-operator pod-watcher reporting the same failure as Test 1 — it's the ci-operator framework's view of the test pod exiting with code 1 (from the git checkout release-. failure). Not a separate failure; it is the ci-operator-level representation of Test 1.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — same as Test 1.
• Source File: ci-operator framework (not in commatrix).
• Is it a flake? yes — same cascade.
• Suggested Fix: Same as Test 1.


TL;DR: Bare metal cluster API (10.1.104.200:64425) unreachable at test start; all 6 steps timed out or failed via cascade.


Relation Between Failures: All 6 failures share a single
